                    }],
                    mapIsMandatory: !1,
                    mapLoading: !1,
                    name: null,
                    email: null,
                    mobile_number: null,
                    address_country_id: null,
                    address_city_id: null,
                    address_street: null,
                    short_address: null,
                    address_district: null,
                    city_name: null,
                    country_code: null,
                    submit_login_progress: !1,
                    submitStatus: null,
                    get_country_cities_progress: !1,
                    quickDonationProductRequest: null,
                    cityMapId: null,

            validations: function() {
                return {
                    name: {
                        required: N.required
                    },
                    email: {
                        email: N.email,
                        required: N.required
                    },
                    mobile_number: {
                        required: N.required,
                        minLength: Object(N.minLength)(8),
                        maxLength: Object(N.maxLength)(14)
                    },
                    address_country_id: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping
                        })
                    },
                    address_city_id: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping
                        })
                    },
                    address_street: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping && this.isFieldActive("street", this.selectedCountryCode) && this.isFieldMandatory("street", this.selectedCountryCode)
                        })
                    },
                    address_district: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping
                        })
                    },
                    city_name: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.isOtherCity
                        })
                    },
                    country_code: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping
                        })
                    },
                    building_number: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.isFieldActive("building_number", this.selectedCountryCode) && this.isFieldMandatory("building_number", this.selectedCountryCode)
                        }),
                        maxLength: !this.isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled && Object(N.maxLength)(8)
                    },
                    additional_number: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.isFieldActive("additional_number", this.selectedCountryCode) && this.isFieldMandatory("additional_number", this.selectedCountryCode)
                        }),
                        maxLength: !this.isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled && Object(N.maxLength)(9)
                    },
                    postcode: {
                        required: Object(N.requiredIf)(function() {
                            return this.requiredShipping && this.isFieldActive("postcode", this.selectedCountryCode) && this.isFieldMandatory("postcode", this.selectedCountryCode)
                        }),
                        maxLength: !this.isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled && Object(N.maxLength)(8)
                    }
                }
            },
            computed: s(s({}, Object(v.b)({
                store: "store/store",
                cart: "cart/cart"
            })), {}, {
                selectedCountryCode: function() {
                    return this.findCountryById(this.address_country_id).code
                },
                countriesValues: function() {
                    return this.$store.getters.countries.map(function(e) {
                        return e.id
                    })
                },
                cityValues: function() {
                    var e = this.getSelectedCountryCities();
                    return e ? e.map(function(e) {
                        return e.id
                    }) : []
                },
                isOtherCity: function() {
                    return !!this.address_city_id && "Other" === this.cityName(this.address_city_id, "en")
                },
                isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled: function() {
                    return this.$store.getters.is_address_intl_updates_enabled
                },
                isCountryKsa: function() {
                    if (this.isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled) {
                        var e = this.findCountryById(this.address_country_id);
                        return e && "SA" === e.code
                    }
                    return "184" == this.address_country_id || "183" == this.address_country_id
                },
                isCountryKW: function() {
                    return "KW" === this.findCountryById(this.address_country_id).code
                },
                isAddtionalFieldsRequired: function() {
                    return this.requiredShipping && !this.isCountryKsa && !this.isIntlAddressUpdateEnabled
                },
                toggleGoogleMaps: function() {
                    return this.$store.state && this.$store.state.store && this.$store.state.store.is_gmaps_in_address_enabled
                },
                toggleSplMaps: function() {
                    return this.$store.state && this.$store.state.store && this.$store.state.store.is_spl_in_address_enabled
                },
                isGoogleMapMandatory: function() {
                    return this.$store.state && this.$store.state.store && this.$store.state.store.is_gmaps_in_address_enabled && this.$store.state.store.is_gmaps_in_address_mandatory
                },
                address: function() {
                    return {
                        formatted_address: this.formatted_address,
                        address_lat: this.editShippingAddress ? this.editShippingAddress.address_lat : null,
                        address_lng: this.editShippingAddress ? this.editShippingAddress.address_lng : null
                    }
                },
                ShippingAddress: function() {
                    return this.cart && this.cart.shipping_address
                },
                checkMultiInventoriesWithSpl: function() {
                    return !this.$store.state.store.has_multi_product_inventory || !this.$store.state.session.deliveryCountry || this.$store.state.session && this.$store.state.session.deliveryCountry == this.address_country_id && this.$store.state.store.has_multi_product_inventory
                },
                IsMandatory: function() {
                    return !!(this.requiredShipping && this.isGoogleMapMandatory && this.location && null == this.location.lat && null == this.location.lng)
                }
            }),
            watch: {
                address_country_id: function(e) {
                    var t = parseInt(e);
                    /^\d+$/.test(e) ? this.address_country_id = t : this.address_country_id = void 0,
                    t && t > 0 && this.fetchCitiesOfCountry(t)
